    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

  <span id="freeText16167819572739676176" style="display:none">Book #2 of the erotic This Man trilogy<br /><br />Jesse Ward drowned her with his intensity and blindsided her with his passion, but he kept her away from his dark secrets and broken soul. Leaving him was the only way Ava O'Shea could survive. She should have known that Jesse Ward is impossible to escape--and now he's back in her life, determined to remind her of the sensual pleasures they had shared. Ava is equally determined to get at the truth beneath this man's steely exterior. That means letting herself get close to the Lord of the Manor once more. And it's exactly where Jesse wants her--within touching distance...</span>

<div id="review_509846688" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/509846688" />
    <a title="Miss H" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15490946-miss-h"><img alt="Miss H" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475977422p2/15490946.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/509846688?book_show_action=true">Jan 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Miss H" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Miss H" href="/user/show/15490946-miss-h">Miss H</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16156709-beneath-this-man">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=needs-proper-editing">needs-proper-editing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=insta-love-or-insta-lust">insta-love-or-insta-lust</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=drama-llama">drama-llama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=hated-this-book">hated-this-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=insufferable-mc">insufferable-mc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=spineless-doormat-heroine">spineless-doormat-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=bored-out-of-my-mind">bored-out-of-my-mind</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=badly-written">badly-written</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=just-plain-awful">just-plain-awful</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer509846688" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8067501054004760805"><b>Warning: spoilers abound.</b><br/><br/>Apparently, I’m a glutton for punishment. Me and this book/trilogy are not friends. Not at all. It's like a train wreck—I don't want to look, but can't stop myself.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/189827.gif' width='400' height='189' alt='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Only five short days have passed since Ava left Jesse, and her entire world has ended. She’s depressed and having a meltdown, reminiscing about her epic love—you know, her month-long relationship with Jesse. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405673i/790609.jpg' width='400' height='294' alt='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Of course, this being only the second book, it stands to reason that their separation won’t last long, </span>
  <span id="freeText8067501054004760805" style="display:none"><b>Warning: spoilers abound.</b><br><br>Apparently, I’m a glutton for punishment. Me and this book/trilogy are not friends. Not at all. It's like a train wreck—I don't want to look, but can't stop myself.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/189827.gif" width="400" height="189" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Only five short days have passed since Ava left Jesse, and her entire world has ended. She’s depressed and having a meltdown, reminiscing about her epic love—you know, her month-long relationship with Jesse. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405673i/790609.jpg" width="400" height="294" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Of course, this being only the second book, it stands to reason that their separation won’t last long, and, just like that, they’re back together. Shocked? Yeah, neither am I.<br><br>Not much has changed. Jesse is still a domineering, overly possessive, control freak…times infinity. He’s a stage-five clinger. He continually wants all of Ava’s time and attention, wanting her to spend every second with him all day, every day. She’s a possession, a toy that he refuses to share. Nothing about this behavior is sexy. It’s scary. Jesse is a psycho. <br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>‘Watch your fucking mouth.’ he yells.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Pot, meet kettle. Kettle, meet pot. Jesse treats Ava as if she were a misbehaving child. Ava is a grown woman. She doesn’t need this man-child correcting her language. As usual, however, Jesse has absolutely no regard for Ava’s feelings. He does want he wants, when he wants. On the other hand, Ava has the backbone of a spineless chicken, so it’s no wonder Jesse tramples all over her.<br><br>Oh, and don’t worry. Jesse’s not an alcoholic.<br><br>Except that he is.<br><br>Alcoholism, or any addiction, really, is a life-long recovery, and something a person has to work hard at every day. It doesn't just simply go away on its own. The narrative would have readers believe that Jesse doesn’t “need” alcohol, ignoring the fact that it was made clear, on more than one occasion, that he can’t stop once he starts. That’s a problem, one made even more apparent when he drinks himself into a coma.<br><br>Unfortunately, everyone in this book is in denial.<br><br><blockquote>1:<i> ‘He’s not an alcoholic in the classic sense of the word. He’s not obsessed with alcohol, Ava. He drank to lighten his foul mood, to fill a gap. Once he starts, he can’t stop.’</i>
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>2:<i> ‘I’m not a raving alcoholic, Ava. I admit I get carried away once I do have a drink and I find it hard to stop, but I can take it or leave it. I was in a bad place after you left me. I just wanted to numb the pain.’</i>
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>3:<i> ‘I am not a fucking alcoholic. If I drink now, it will be because you make me crazy mad!’ He shouts the last bit in my face.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>And then, of course, Ava puts the blame on herself.<br><br><blockquote>1:<i> I glance at the bottle and notice it’s sealed and full, but it’s still there and something made him put it there…me. I’m the reason for his screwed up mind, his ridiculously ambitious objectives and his meltdowns. This is my entire fault. I’ve made him into a neurotic control freak.</i>
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>2:<i> ‘How can you need me if I make you do this to yourself?’ I ask tiredly. ‘You’re more self-destructible now than you were before me. I’ve made you need alcohol, not want it. I’ve made you into an unreasonable, crazy man, and I’m certainly not stable anymore. Don’t you see what we’re doing to each other?’</i>
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>3:<i> I blank my mind of everything except that, the music fades and I brace myself for my own punishment – my punishment for reducing Jesse to a fraught mess of a man, for making him need alcohol, not just want it, for turning him into an uptight, neurotic freak…for making him do this to himself.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>That last quote was from a scene that made me rage. In an idiotic bid to get Jesse see her point of view, Ava has some random man at the Manor whip her back raw—you know, the same way that Jesse had Sarah whip his. Why would he go to Sarah with such a request, you might ask? The answer is simple: to stop himself from drinking. But, wait, he doesn’t have a problem, remember?<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>‘Nothing will ever hurt me as much as seeing you doing that to yourself. That will kill me, nothing else. If you punish yourself again, then I will too.’</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405673ra/790610.gif" width="400" height="224" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>These two idiots deserve each other. Truly. <br><br>As if we didn’t already know, Jesse is <s>secretly</s> trying to knock Ava up—against her wishes, no less—to trap her into staying with him. He makes her tell him repeatedly that she won’t leave him, not that he’d ever let her, but her word isn’t assurance enough for him. Because Jesse is an insecure lunatic, his solution is to bring a baby into their dysfunctional and extremely unhealthy relationship. Brining a baby into an environment like that is outrageous. Even after Ava finally puts the pieces together, she lets it slide, just like everything else. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398275ra/769552.gif" width="400" height="204" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397298ra/766464.gif" width="400" height="204" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I didn’t think it was possible, but I stand corrected. Ava is an even bigger pushover than she was in the last book. Arguing with Jesse is a complete waste of time. She gives in as soon as he gets his hands on her. Jesse is a bully and tramples all over her. She knows this, and still, unbelievably, allows it to happen. I just can’t with her. She’s a moron. <br><br>Jesse is also guilty of the following, none of which are even remotely okay: hiding Ava’s birth control pills, using sex as a weapon to get what he wants, and invading and taking control of Ava's personal and professional life. This doesn’t even begin to cover all the lying and manipulation, both in and out of the bedroom. Oh, and we can add cheating to the list, as well.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405673ra/790611.gif" width="400" height="224" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And then there’s Kate. Who needs enemies when you have a friend like her? I’m sorry, but she’s a terrible friend. She’s secretive, willing to hide things from her so-called best friend on Jesse’s behalf—information that pertains to Jesse and his private life—not because she knows that Jesse is a good guy, but because he bought her a new work van to keep her quiet about what she knows about the kind of business he operates. <br><br>I wans't a fan of the writing. It was pedestrian and bland. The book could also use a good editor. Almost all the dialogue tags were punctuated incorrectly, with periods at the end of the dialogue where commas should've been used instead. I'm of the opinion that if one is going to put their book out on the market for people to buy, then it should be properly edited.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>His eyes turn black. ‘Don’t say things like that, Ava.’</i>
</blockquote><br><br>When did this turn into a paranormal romance? Human eyes do not turn black when one is angry. Just saying.<br><br>Sex, fighting, and more sex. That's about all this book had to offer. We did eventually learn how old Jesse was. Not that it mattered, because he sure as hell didn't act his age. He was prone to acting like an adolescent. We also learned some things about his past sexual encounters. <i>‘Drink and sex go hand in hand for me.’</i> So, as you can see, alcohol wasn't his only problem. As far as any real plot progression went, that was the extent of it. In between the excessive amount of sex scenes, there wasn't much of a story at all.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8067501054004760805" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer460157819" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5772427394737323360">This book is now live on Amazon everyone!! Full review, finally posted!!<br/><br/> <a href='http://www.amazon.com/Beneath-This-Man-Trilogy-ebook/dp/B00B1WP8T4/ref=sr_1_2?s=digital-text&ie=UTF8&qid=1358410655&sr=1-2' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon.com</a> <a href='http://www.amazon.co.uk/Beneath-This-Man-Trilogy-ebook/dp/B00B1WP8T4/ref=sr_1_2?s=digital-text&ie=UTF8&qid=1358414829&sr=1-2' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon UK</a><br/><b>
  <blockquote>
<br/>I want the woman with me who keeps my heart beating.</blockquote>
</b><br/><a href='http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/2013/01/beneath-this-man-by-jodi-ellen.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398284i/769562.jpg' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>Wow! Just, Wow!</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/>Before you read my review, please just open <a href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=hbe3CQamF8k' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Massive Attack’s Angel</a> in a new window and play it in the background as you read.  This song features frequently during the book and is Jesse’s song for Ava.  Play it<strong> LOUD</strong>!<br/><br/>This has to be one of the most anticipated releases of 2013. After the last desperate and devastating few chapt</span>
  <span id="freeText5772427394737323360" style="display:none">This book is now live on Amazon everyone!! Full review, finally posted!!<br><br> <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Beneath-This-Man-Trilogy-ebook/dp/B00B1WP8T4/ref=sr_1_2?s=digital-text&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1358410655&amp;sr=1-2" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon.com</a> <a href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/Beneath-This-Man-Trilogy-ebook/dp/B00B1WP8T4/ref=sr_1_2?s=digital-text&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1358414829&amp;sr=1-2" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon UK</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>
<br>I want the woman with me who keeps my heart beating.</blockquote>
</b><br><a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/2013/01/beneath-this-man-by-jodi-ellen.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398284i/769562.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Wow! Just, Wow!</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Before you read my review, please just open <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=hbe3CQamF8k" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Massive Attack’s Angel</a> in a new window and play it in the background as you read.  This song features frequently during the book and is Jesse’s song for Ava.  Play it<strong> LOUD</strong>!<br><br>This has to be one of the most anticipated releases of 2013. After the last desperate and devastating few chapters of This Man, we’ve all been waiting with bated breath for more Jesse &amp; Ava. The second book of a trilogy is traditionally the weakest, it’s neither a beginning or an end and can often be just filler but that is NOT the case here. This book just blew me away, I <b>DEVOURED</b> it and I am now bereft that it is over and can’t wait for the third book to be able to finally conclude this intense and overwhelming romance.<br><br>We left Jesse &amp; Ava in the depths of despair at the end of This Man. Both of them are broken by what has happened and their relationship is seemingly in ruins. They’re both in pieces and wrecked and, Jesse especially, hell-bent on self-destruction. This was done so very well – their broken hearts and intense overwhelming sadness leap vividly to life right off the page and their despair is palpable. They’re just lost without each other.<br><br>As they move beyond these events and attempt to get their relationship back on track I couldn’t help feel that their connection was one of the most intense and most emotional that I think I’ve ever read in romantic fiction. I so wanted them to sort out their differences, to be open and honest with each other and to find that Happy Ever After that’s constantly drifting ever so slightly out of reach. I read with a big grin, loving every minute that they were together and then again always with that ever-present worry that Jodi Ellen Malpas was going to rip the rug out from under us with some unforeseen complication and plummet them back down into the darkness. It’s a story of unbelievably wonderful highs followed by despondent lows. <br><br>Jesse is back in all his arrogant, alpha, dominant controlling glory with sleepy sex, sense fucks, reminder fucks and now even retribution fucks. The steam factor in this book is off the charts <b>HAWT!!</b> <br><br> The normally strong dominant playboy has been reduced to a frightened desperate soul by the intensity and depth of his feelings for Ava. He’s lived a hedonistic lifestyle until the moment he met her, he’s never cared for the multitude of women that he’s had physical relationships with and was fairly self-destructive not caring whether he lived or died. Now Ava has burst onto his horizon and he can hardly see straight, he loves her so much. He’s terrified that he’s going to lose her, that someone will take her from him and she brings out all his extremely over-protective instincts. He’s a troublesome, neurotic rogue and there were times that I wanted to scream at him, bang his head against a brick wall to knock some sense into him – he made me crazy. Ava too. I was just rooting for them to find a happy balance – an equilibrium that would ultimately ease their troubled souls but they’re so deeply connected to one another, body and soul, they have the power to absolutely destroy one other.<br><br> Ava continues to be a wonderful heroine that you can truly believe in. She’s as overwhelmed as Jesse by her feelings and is completely bowled over by him. She’s a feisty soul and despite Jesse’s dominant presence manages to win some of their battles. She’s strong and independent and doesn’t take well to Jesse trying to micro-manage her life to the nth degree and it makes for a tortuous path as they argue and dispute every little aspect of their life together only to make up with seriously hot <b>off the charts</b> steamy bedroom action! Ava feels a connection to Jesse that she has never felt with anyone ever before and he makes her ecstatically happy and allows her to feel safe at the same time as driving her totally barking mad.<br><br> Beneath This Man is a beautiful, captivating, conflicting, tortuous romance that had me completely consumed by their story. I was totally absorbed by the words on the page, everything else just faded into the background as I lost myself absolutely in their fictional world, falling more and more in love with Jesse with every chapter. There’s just something so open and engaging about what is passing between them. It’s also funny as we get to see the little quirks of character from This Man building and growing giving you the reader a feeling that you’re getting to know this central duo so very well. They feel like friends. There’s also a great host of secondary characters with poor Clive, the much abused concierge at Lusso, John an absolute pillar of strength at The Manor and Kate and Sam and all of Ava’s riotous friends and colleagues.<br><br> As I was lucky enough to be one of the earliest to read this, I got asked over and over the same questions – how old is Jesse, how did he get that scar, did he sleep with Sarah, and more. All I can say is – you’re just going to have to read the book. I know you’re all desperate to know but you don’t really want me to tell you. You’ll want to experience it for yourself just the way the author intended.<br><br>So, this was my first 5 star read of 2013 and an absolutely stunning continuation of the This Man trilogy and I can’t wait to get my hands on book 3. If you liked This Man, you’re going to absolutely love Beneath This Man. If you enjoy your romance on the angsty, emotional and intense side then this book is most definitely for you.<br><br> 5 stars super steamy and very special erotic romance<br><br><br><a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/2013/01/beneath-this-man-by-jodi-ellen.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398284i/769563._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>ARC courtesy of Jodi Ellen Malpas with thanks<br><br>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a> or visit us on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sinfullysexybookreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>.</i></span>

What mystery was unraveled?</b><br>Well.. His age, we learned about his scar question, about his past &amp; how he got The Manor, about his affairs and sordid ex-life. No one enjoys reading that much only about sex and nothing else. I felt like there was no story. Irritating lil bitch. I mean woman, stop being so bloody hyper like a crazy kid on sugar. AND calm the fuck down for heavens sake!<br><br>She's like all<br><i>'OH He's shaking, Is he having withdrawal symptoms'</i><br>Like sure crazy, just after 5 days.<br><br><i>'OMG, He had 3 bottles of Vodka, He's an alcoholic.. need to send him for AA'</i><br>Hell woman! Nothing.’</b> - Jesse</i> <br><br><i><b>‘I want the woman with me who keeps my heart beating.’</b> - Jesse</i> Awwieeeee <i>*gushes*</i><br><br><b>35%</b> in, I seriously feel like I'm reading a Mystery Erotica than a Romantic Erotica!<br><br><b>37%</b> in the book, I am literally laughing at the absurdity of events!! I MEAN c'mon, you don't do that so someone. Its like using sex to get your ways.         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer489155223" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer950253513338206554"><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/MalpasBeneathThisMan2TitlebySueBee_zps6523eeb4.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402577i/782578.jpg' alt=' photo MalpasBeneathThisMan2TitlebySueBee_zps6523eeb4.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Heroes/1310_1eea_480-gif_zps6a4201a4.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386128899ra/7297219.gif' alt=' photo 1310_1eea_480-gif_zps6a4201a4.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>★★★★★! Beneath This Man, book 2 of 3. The continuation of the in control yet so out-of-control, Jesse Ward’s intense whirlwind romance with Ava O’Shea!</b><br/><br/><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I look up into his green eyes and wisely note that he’s not in a fucking about mood. I want to bring to his attention that I’m not happy about his evasion of my enquiry, but I know it will get me entirely nowhere right now. Besides, I’m absolutely delighted to see my domineering man back. It’s been too long.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br/><b>This M</b></span>
  <span id="freeText950253513338206554" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/MalpasBeneathThisMan2TitlebySueBee_zps6523eeb4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402577i/782578.jpg" alt=" photo MalpasBeneathThisMan2TitlebySueBee_zps6523eeb4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Heroes/1310_1eea_480-gif_zps6a4201a4.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386128899ra/7297219.gif" alt=" photo 1310_1eea_480-gif_zps6a4201a4.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>★★★★★! Beneath This Man, book 2 of 3. The continuation of the in control yet so out-of-control, Jesse Ward’s intense whirlwind romance with Ava O’Shea!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I look up into his green eyes and wisely note that he’s not in a fucking about mood. I want to bring to his attention that I’m not happy about his evasion of my enquiry, but I know it will get me entirely nowhere right now. Besides, I’m absolutely delighted to see my domineering man back. It’s been too long.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>This Man Series is the intense, epic saga about Jesse Ward</b>, Mr. Sexy, Bossy, Compulsive and Secretive Extraordinaire, <b>in his relentless pursuit and seduction of interior designer, Ava O’Shea</b>. Their story is filled with covert pasts and hidden agendas! It’s truly a wild, bumpy and emotional ride loaded with intrigue and shockers, undiluted lust and mind-bending sex plus a compulsive and intense love. Be prepared to be swept away by their story!<br><br><u>Books in This Man series should be read in order:</u><br><b>Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/484476053" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">This Man</a><br>Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/489155223" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Beneath This Man</a><br>Book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/509586014" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">This Man Confessed</a><br>Book 4: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2137108028" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">With This Man</a></b><br><br><b>Beneath This Man (book 2)</b> picks up just days after the shocking cliff-hanger ending of book 1. Jesse and Ava have lots to overcome and uncover. For starters <b>Jesse’s secrets and compulsive need to control and Eva’s desperate struggle not to be swallowed by everything that is Jesse</b>, faltering between needing and demanding to know and not standing up enough for herself. Add to that their intense, co-dependent feelings and addictive sexual attraction and throw in <b>vindictive villains, surprises and set-backs</b> and you have a heck of a roller-coaster. Strap on your seatbelts, or should I say handcuff yourself to something…<br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/MalpasThisMan1-2HerobySueBee_zpse1eafa65.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401889i/780597.jpg" alt=" photo MalpasThisMan1-2HerobySueBee_zpse1eafa65.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Jesse Ward</b> is just what I needed. In fact he is everything I needed! He truly is all pure, sexy, unadulterated bossy alpha!<br><br>Six words to describe <b>Jesse: Intense, bossy, compulsive, enigmatic, possessive and elusive.</b><br><br>I’d also like to extend my sincere thanks for introducing us to <b>all that is sex with Jesse</b> (or fucks depending on the mood):<br><b>
  <i>Reminder fucks, Sleepy sex, Make friends sex, Shower fucks, Hangover sex, Catching up sex, Sense fucks, Seeing stars fucks, Apology fucks, Possessive fucks, Retribution fucks, Sleepy celebration sex… <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Proposal fucks and… Truth fucks. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> The last one courtesy Ava.</i>
</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Watch your mouth. I pissed on your plan?’ he asks incredulously. ‘Ava, let me tell you, nowhere in my plan was it written that you would have me restrained and at your mercy. So, it is you who pissed all over my plan.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/MalpasThisMan1-3HeroinebySueBee_zpsc735a4ac.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401889i/780598.jpg" alt=" photo MalpasThisMan1-3HeroinebySueBee_zpsc735a4ac.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Ava O’Shea</b> is everything that Jesse needed and everything we needed to keep the story going. She stood up to him, she succumbed to him, she riled him, she created more drama and she kept the mystery and story going by NOT demanding answers. <br><br>Six words to describe <b>Ava; Talented, strong, focused, ambitious, stubborn and meek.</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“He’s fighting a grin. ‘I am confident, because you said yes. Or was it…’ He looks up to the ceiling in deep thought and then back at me. ‘Oh, I remember. It was… yes, yes, yes, fucking hell, yes!</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>Euphoric Angst! Intense! Epic! Captivating! I am so thankful to Ms. Malpas!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Kiss me, now.’ he demands, and I dive straight in with an appreciation kiss. He’s opened up and I feel so much better. Basking on Central Jesse cloud nine has resumed.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>As I’m coming down from all that is <b>“Central Jesse Cloud Nine”</b> I find myself staring into space. What an a.m.a.z.i.n.g. read! I think I am going to need some sense knocked back into me – seriously! <b>Jesse. Jesse! JESSE! JESSSEEEE!</b> Ugh, actually what I need is book 3, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/509586014" rel="nofollow noopener">This Man Confessed</a>. What a relief it’s about to be released! <b>Three… Two… ONE… ZEROOO!!!</b><br><br>***<br>Hero rating: 5+ stars <br>Heroine rating: 5 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 5 stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 5 stars<br>Storyline concept rating: 5 stars<br>Storyline execution rating: 5 stars<br>Storytelling skills rating: 5 stars<br>Story ending rating: N/A<br>*********************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 5 stars<br><br>Would I recommend this series: Yes.<br>Would I re-read this series: Yes!<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS/2lSrB_zps64bb8ed8.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402578ra/782579.gif" alt=" photo 2lSrB_zps64bb8ed8.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_537547722" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/537547722" />
    <a title="Tina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16458477-tina"><img alt="Tina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1606198430p2/16458477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/537547722?book_show_action=true">Feb 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tina" href="/user/show/16458477-tina">Tina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16156709-beneath-this-man">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">nobody</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16458477-tina?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer537547722" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10694432692968629824">I don't know if there was a deep hidden message in this book, you know, some kind of deep meaning that I didn't get. But if there were, I could only come to the conclusion that my brain isn't developed enough to comprehend the value of it.<br/><br/>Let me tell you what I do know. I now know why the author chose the name <i>Beneath this man</i>, and it's because this 'story' is about a man walking all over a girl's life, self-esteem and dignity and ripping every ounce of rational thought out of her head (and I do</span>
  <span id="freeText10694432692968629824" style="display:none">I don't know if there was a deep hidden message in this book, you know, some kind of deep meaning that I didn't get. But if there were, I could only come to the conclusion that my brain isn't developed enough to comprehend the value of it.<br /><br />Let me tell you what I do know. I now know why the author chose the name <i>Beneath this man</i>, and it's because this 'story' is about a man walking all over a girl's life, self-esteem and dignity and ripping every ounce of rational thought out of her head (and I don't mean it in the good way). This woman has literally put her life <i>
  <b>beneath</b>
</i> her 'feelings' for this man, a man that deserves nothing else but to be left to rot in a pile of flesh-eating bugs.<br /><br />Even though this book is completely plotless and filled with crappy dialogues, there is a great variety when it comes to humiliation and abuse. At the very beginning of the series we have this girl who is portrayed to be relatively normal--you know, she is young, she is fairly successful in what she does. Yes, she is out of a bad relationship, but haven't we all been like that at some point? Then this guy comes along and smashes everything for her. He literally takes her life away from her by dickmatizing her--he makes her a slave to the cock, girls, and you know it.<br /><br />But it gets even better in <i>Beneath this man</i>. He is literally telling her how she is supposed to live her life. He wants her around him all the time, so that he can fucking control every damn second of her life. And if he were reading this, he would simply say <i>'Watch your fucking mouth!'</i><br /><br />Now, probably every girl on this planet loves the alpha-male and/or the bad boy. Women just feel the need to be protected, you know--it's pretty natural and I accept it. What I cannot accept, however, is how on earth is it possible for women to like this book altogether. This is a book about a woman being ordered around, told and forced what to do, not about a woman who is loved. And if you still think that you are about to read a love story, you should simply get it out of your heads. This is not love; this is all about a girl becoming obsessed with a guy's dick. And even though a lot of Jesse's actions are explained through his supposed love to Ava, I cannot feel the love in the air. What I feel is a woman's desperation to be with a person who is manipulating her with sex. To be honest, I was very happy when she somehow grasped it at one point, but unfortunately this insight didn't last long. <br /><br />I think that I could best describe this book by using the author's own words:<br /><br /><i>'My sanity is certainly questionable, but I'm sane enough to admit that. I was a normal, sound-minded girl. I definitely don't qualify for that anymore.'</i><br /><br />To sum it up--no self-respecting woman that is sane, not under chemically induced coma or drugged should like this book. Because liking this book automatically means that you would enjoy going through all of the shit described in this book. Oh yeah, and then rate it 5 stars.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10694432692968629824" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3227564736783788740">I don't know why for the life of me I keep reading these books, I must be sick in the head. Reading these two books is like exploring the mind of a certified nut job, how can any woman think this shit is romantic or better yet sexy?<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405793i/791032.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Jesse, oh Jesse, here's a tip, just cause you deny you're an alcoholic doesn't make it true. Guess what? YOU'RE A FUCKING ALCOHOLIC ! I don't care how you dress it up, you have a problem and blaming other people for your actions is just stupid. No one forced that bott</span>
  <span id="freeText3227564736783788740" style="display:none">I don't know why for the life of me I keep reading these books, I must be sick in the head. Reading these two books is like exploring the mind of a certified nut job, how can any woman think this shit is romantic or better yet sexy?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405793i/791032.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jesse, oh Jesse, here's a tip, just cause you deny you're an alcoholic doesn't make it true. Guess what? YOU'RE A FUCKING ALCOHOLIC ! I don't care how you dress it up, you have a problem and blaming other people for your actions is just stupid. No one forced that bottle of booze in your hand, that was all you. I honestly don't understand how Ava can go back to someone who is nothing more than a brash, overbearing, emotionally unstable, sex addict, and all around asshole, of a man. I kept waiting for him to install a GPS chip on her ass, he didn't even give her privacy in the toilet for peets sake! Yes, he loves her, that's nice, so whats more even more romantic than a declaration of love, ah yes a proposal mid-fuck. What girl wouldn't swoon over that move, here's what I have to say to that:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405793ra/791033.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What's more annoying than Jesse is Ava, she just lets him continuously push her around. Not only him but his friends too, after being wrangled into checking on Jesse she stays to take care of him. Uh, let his fucking friends do that shit, you don't owe him anything. Ava eventually relents and continues her relationship with the psycho but its anything but healthy. He forces her into situations she is clearly uncomfortable with and its painful to read. Every time she "stands her ground" she ends up relenting in a hot minute, and is on her back in less time than that. She finally wises up to his motives regarding her birth control pills but it was more of a slap on the wrist than anything. Ava, please for the love of God, run for the hills and don't look back.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405793ra/791034.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don't know how the rest of the trilogy will play out, but I know that it will most likely end with me being frustrated and ready to punch someone. I can only hope that if anyone meets a real life Jesse Ward they turn around and walk the other way, no sex is worth all the shit that goes along with a crazy.<br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4914501980705089160"><br/><b>Well...<br/><br/>To be honest, I've never been <i>this close</i> to getting a headache while reading a book as I was with this one...<br/><br/>Seriously, this is one of the most frustrating and exhausting books I've EVER read.</b><br/><br/><p><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380352896ra/706299.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Review might contain spoilers for those who haven't read This Man yet...</i><br/><br/><b><u>Ava and Jesse's relationship in a nutshell:</u></b><br/><br/>♦ Ava and Jesse driving each other C.R.A.Z.Y.<br/><br/>♦ Jesse hiding Ava's birth control pills.<br/><br/>♦ Sex, lots of sex in all the different forms including:<br/> ♢ Retribution f*ck<br/> ♢ Apology f*ck<br/> ♢ Truth f</p></span>
  <span id="freeText4914501980705089160" style="display:none"><br><b>Well...<br><br>To be honest, I've never been <i>this close</i> to getting a headache while reading a book as I was with this one...<br><br>Seriously, this is one of the most frustrating and exhausting books I've EVER read.</b><br><br><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380352896ra/706299.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Review might contain spoilers for those who haven't read This Man yet...</i><br><br><b><u>Ava and Jesse's relationship in a nutshell:</u></b><br><br>♦ Ava and Jesse driving each other C.R.A.Z.Y.<br><br>♦ Jesse hiding Ava's birth control pills.<br><br>♦ Sex, lots of sex in all the different forms including:<br> ♢ Retribution f*ck<br> ♢ Apology f*ck<br> ♢ Truth f*ck<br> ♢ Sense f*ck<br> ♢ Sleepy sex<br> ♢ Celebration sex<br><br>♦ Three...two...one...zero, baby. -&gt; Jesse giving Ava "The Countdown".<br><br>♦ Jesse telling Ava to <i>"watch her fucking mouth"</i> whenever she sweares.<br><br>♦ Jesse refusing to tell Ava his real age <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[until a certain morning where Ava gets creative and manages to make him confess his age  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br>♦ Women from Jesse's past trying to tear them apart in order to get him back.<br><br>♦ Ava being on Central Jesse Cloud Nine.<br><br><b>End of.</b><br></p><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401656ra/779868.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Despite the fact that this book mentally exhausted me like no other book ever has, I did find myself spellbound by Ava and Jesse's unique and dramatic love life and I was unable to stop reading their over-the-top crazy story. Eventually, I really did end up liking the second part of this trilogy much more than the first one.<br><br>Except for Ava...<br><br>OMG, Ava...<br></p><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401656ra/779869.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There were soooo many times where I wanted to yell at her to get her head out of the sand and to stop being so naïve. She made me want to pull my hair out every time she let Jesse trample all over her BUT, luckily, she did start to stand up for herself more towards the ending. So there's still hope for her yet.<br><br>And then there's Jesse and his ever domineering and controlling ways...<br></p><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401656ra/779870.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I mean, it can't possibly be healthy to be <i>this</i> possessive and obsessed, right!?<br><br></p><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You're mine, and mine alone, baby. Just for my eyes, just for my touch and just for my pleasure. Just mine. Do you understand me?"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Jesse pretty much takes "crazy obsessed and controlling" to a whole new level, which would drive any other sane woman insane. And although it drives Ava insane too, she manages to challenge him in other ways which makes them complement each other perfectly.<br><br>And it's kind of hard not to fall for Jesse when he's saying things like this...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I can't believe you're in my life. I can't believe you're mine. You are so, so precious to me, baby."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>And this... <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <blockquote>
    <b>
      <i>"You completely consume me, Ava. I can't function without you. I'm totally addicted to you, baby." His voice is soft and unsure. My confident, domineering ex-playboy is nervous. "You own me. Marry me."</i>
    </b>
  </blockquote>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>*SWOON*<br><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401656ra/779871.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So yeah, even though Ava and Jesse drive each other crazy mad sometimes, it's also obvious that they're crazy in love and I can't wait to find out how their story continues. (After I've taken a mental breather, that is, because I'm sure there's a lot more drama and craziness to come...). <br><br><br><b>♦ 3.5-ish STARS ♦</b></p></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

Beneath this Man left off right where This Man ended. 5 days since Ava has seen Jesse. They are both broken. They are both a mess.   <span id="freeText14083702516601077111" style="display:none"><br><b>5 Central Jesse Cloud Nine, Crazy Mad Stars!!!</b><br><br>Where to begin... Beneath this Man left off right where This Man ended. 5 days since Ava has seen Jesse. They are both broken. They are both a mess. They both realize that the need each other. <br><br><b>Jesse Ward- you are crazy beautiful, crazy mad, crazy possessive, crazy in love, crazy sexy... key word... CRAZY! </b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/albums/y537/Christyb23/?action=view&amp;current=JESSEWARD1-1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379784459i/457760.jpg" alt="Jesse Ward" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Lord of the Sex Manor.<br>Mr. Challenging. Domineering. Alpha male.<br>Sexy as hell. Sweet. ‘Easy going’ lol<br><br>Jesse was much more likable in this book than in the first. To be completely honest, I liked this book much more than the first! Jesse was a little crazy, as I’m sure we’ve established. Jesse has come a long way. He is not perfect, but he’s trying to heal. We learned a lot more about Jesse and his past in this book, though he still has a little mystery left. Loved that we finally found out Jesse’s age! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ “I’m thirty seven! For fucks sake woman, I’m thirty fucking seven!” <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Some of Jesse’s favorite lines... <br><b>
  <i>“Ava, this is not up for discussion. End of.”<br>“Always in Lace.” <br>“We’re going to make friends.”<br>“Three.. Two... One... Zero.”<br>“Ava, watch your mouth.”<br>“Ava, will you watch your fucking mouth!” <br>“MOUTH!”<br>“For God’s sake, Ava stop swearing!”<br>“Will you stop fucking swearing?”</i>

With lots and lots of sex: <b>Sleepy sex, sleepy celebration sex, reminder fucking, retribution sex, sense fucking, the list goes on and on</b> But it was hot!!! 100% steamy and sexy!<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/albums/y537/Christyb23/?action=view&amp;current=JESSEANDAVA.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“It’s just my fucking luck that I go and fall crazy in love with the most impossible woman.”</i>
</b> I like Ava, I do. She drove me a little more crazy at time during the story than Jesse did! I wish she would have more of a backbone with Jesse, but I could see how it would be hard to say no to him.<br><br>The story was great, then at around the 85% mark... <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/albums/y537/Christyb23/?action=view&amp;current=SHITJUSTGOTREAL.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

Really hate that lady but I was never so happy as when Ava hit her and put her in her place! Thats right :D  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/albums/y537/Christyb23/?action=view&amp;current=HESMINEBITCH.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398405i/769928.jpg" alt="beneath this man" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Best. Line. Ever. <b>
  <i>“You EVER lay a finger on him again, requested or not, and I won’t stop until I’ve snapped every bone in your fucking body. Do you understand me?”</i>
</b><br><br>I am really excited for the next book, but a little nervous. I loved the ending and I’m worried things will change. But I’m sure it will be awesome and answer some questions we still have. ..<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/albums/y537/Christyb23/?action=view&amp;current=YOUAREMINE.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398405i/769929.jpg" alt="beneath this man" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>“You’re mine, and mind alone, baby. Just for my eyes, just for my touch and just for my pleasure. Just mine. Do you understand me?” He withdraws and slowly plunges back in. “What about you? Are you just mine?” I ask, shifting my hips up to capture the delightful penetration. <br>“Just yours, Ava. Tell me you love me.”<br>“What?” I cry, when he hits me with a hard drive. <br>“You heard me.” he says softly. “Don’t make me fuck it out of you, baby.”</i>
</b><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/823185621?book_show_action=true">Jan 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shell The Belle " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shell The Belle " href="/user/show/15880350-shell-the-belle">Shell The Belle </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">No-one ever</span></div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer823185621" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1923688418190266538"><b>Review of <i>Beneath This Man</i> by Jodi Ellen Malpas</b><br/><br/><b>1 Star - and that is only for the first few chapters.</b> (<i>For an explanation of my rating system, see my profile)</i><br/><br/><b>A word to trolls, would be trolls and anyone else who disagrees with me; This is my review; It is about how I felt whilst reading and after reading these books. It has no bearing on what you felt about them. It is my opinion. That is all. I am as entitled to my opinion as you are to yours. If you vehemently disagree with my review, that is y</b></span>
  <span id="freeText1923688418190266538" style="display:none"><b>Review of <i>Beneath This Man</i> by Jodi Ellen Malpas</b><br><br><b>1 Star - and that is only for the first few chapters.</b> (<i>For an explanation of my rating system, see my profile)</i><br><br><b>A word to trolls, would be trolls and anyone else who disagrees with me; This is my review; It is about how I felt whilst reading and after reading these books. It has no bearing on what you felt about them. It is my opinion. That is all. I am as entitled to my opinion as you are to yours. If you vehemently disagree with my review, that is your opinion. If you love these books, say so on your review(s) <br><br>DO NOT COMMENT NASTILY ON MY REVIEW SIMPLY BECAUSE YOU DISAGREE – YOU WILL BE FLAGGED AND REPORTED. I WOULD NEVER COMMENT NEGATIVELY ON FIVE STAR ETC REVIEWS OF THESE BOOKS EVEN THOUGH I DISAGREE WITH THEM, SO PLEASE SHOW ME THE SAME COURTESY HERE.<br><br>EVERYONE HAS DIFFERENT OPINIONS AND THEY ARE ALL VALID TO EACH PERSON.</b><br><br><b>
  <u>This book is offensive to Women, and Men, who are real Men. Jesse is <u>NOT </u>a sexy Alpha Male. He is a clingy, whiny insecure controlling bastard.</u>
</b> <br><br>There is not a lot else I can say about this book that I didn’t already say in my review of the first book. Nothing much changes. The characters don’t grow in any way, and they still argue and shout at each other all the damn time it really does give you a headache just reading it., and they still have loads and loads of boring bland sex.<br><br>There is still no real chemistry between Jesse and Ava, and Jesse still continues his over the top controlling ways whilst Ava lets him. Complains about it all the time, but lets him. <br><br>To be honest, if I hadn’t purchased all three books together, having fallen for the hype about these books, I wouldn’t even bother reading book three. <br><br>At the end of the book 1, having been in a rage most of the time reading it, I actually thought there might be a spark of hope for Jesse. We saw him drunk and alone, out of control, still blaming Ava for everything, <i>
  <b>but we saw what I thought was <u>vulnerability.</u> I liked that. I was intrigued.</b>
</i> So I read book two.<br><br><b>Yea, well, that vulnerable side of Jesse? Lasted a few chapters. Done. Back to being arrogant, selfish and over the top control freak.</b><br><br>What I really do not get is why so many people think Jesse is <i>sexy</i>?? I mean I get that he is good looking, fit, has a big dick, and not forgetting fantastically wealthy – but he is nothing more than an arrogant twat. <br><br>Lord of the Manor?? Lord Twattybollocks more like. <br><br><b>Let’s not forget this is the man who cut up Ava’s brand new £500 dress in front of her because he thinks it’s too short/sexy. Yep. What a keeper he is. Dead Romantic. Of course, <i>of course,</i> he only does this because he loves Ava so much, right?</b><br><br>Bullshit.<br><br>Anyone who thinks it would be fab to <i>loved</i> like this, go get yourself some self-respect. This is not love, it is obsession, it is controlling and the guy is the biggest kind of insecure you can get. <br><br>The next thing you know a man like this would be getting your underwear checked to make sure you weren’t cheating.<br><br><i>
  <b>If you really want to know how this would play out, go read the prologue of Axel (Corps Security #1) by Harper Sloan. This is the reality facing someone in Ava’s position in just a few short years.</b>
</i><br><br>Anyway, Ava says over and over again in her mind (but never to Jesse) that this is totally obsessive and controlling over the top behavior, but do you know what? She obviously likes it. Despite her attempt at objecting, she bloody loves it – <b>
  <i>she must do, or she would get the fuck out of that relationship!!</i>
</b><br><br><b>Watch your mouth, Shell The Belle!! </b>Yep, we have a load more of the same stuff as in book one, Jesse constantly swearing, Ava swears back, Jesse tells her to watch her fucking mouth. They argue, they have sex, over and over again - seriously, you will be skipping through the sex bits they are all the same trope. – Ava says she is standing her ground this time then 20 seconds later she is on her back and just giving in – <b>
  <i>Déjà vu much!!</i>
</b><br><br>Ava is even scared at the prospect of introducing Jesse to her parents because she knows he will likely trample on them. Ugh.<br><br><b>Then at around 60% it all goes really stupid.</b> Jesse gives Ava a walking tour of <s>The Bates Motel</s> The Manor, whilst everything is in full swing (pun intended) and I just for life of me can’t see what the hell this woman is still doing with this seedy disgusting guy???<br><br>And then it goes really stupid. Seriously, at around 80% it goes beyond ridiculous. Jesse, unable it seems to stop himself drinking; <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[gets Sarah to whip him as punishment for wanting to drink. Ava walks in on this, and as a punishment to herself, because she now firmly believes that all this is her fault, just as Jesse has been telling her along, she takes herself off to the Communal room and gets a strange man to whip her.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Oh, Fu*king Brilliant. <br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2iqilph" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389706746ra/8049846.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>You both really do deserve each other. Better you stay together rather than spoil anybody else you both might meet. Just don’t blinking breed, for love of . . .<br><br>Talking of which, Ava is still a dumbass and still hasn’t really acknowledged that Jesse is hiding her birth control pills. Oh, about that, does Jesse really think that having a baby together would be a good thing?? They have only known each other a month - a fecking month!! The <b>only</b> thing they have going for them is the sex. And as any couple will tell you, with a baby around there is not much time for much of that!! <br><br>I give up.<br><br>I could go on and show examples of more stupidity, but I’ve wasted enough time on this book as it is. <br><br><b>EDIT:<br>Just a few things I thought I ought to add. <br>One of the reasons I despise this book is the way Jesse treats Ava like a petulant child. He even counts her down from three to zero if she doesn’t do what he wants! And she lets him???<br><br><i>Again, ladies, how the hell is that sexy or romantic?</i><br><br>The character of Ava is not only stupid, but it is completely hollow. She is nothing but a receptacle for Jesse’s (very big) dick. <br><br>I actually thought the character of Jesse Ward had potential; But what he needed was a strong female MC who would challenge his behaviour and dish out a bit of fire herself. Someone who would bring him to his knees if need be. Instead, the character of Ava ruined it completely for me, and I was just left wondering what the hell Jesse saw in her? In essence, these books <i>could</i> have been great. <i>Could have.</i> <br><br>Oh, and I forgot to mention, when Ava’s parents find out that she <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[and Jesse are getting married, <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> are they at all concerned that she has only known him little more than a month???? No, of course not. He is a millionaire, after all. At least that’s the only reason I can see for them having no objections to this ridiculous scenario.<br><br>And about that; they have only known each other around 6 weeks, and in that time they have mainly barked and argued and fought. Yes they have had lots (and lots and lots) of sex, but they have mainly argued, to the point where they split up and Jesse drunk himself almost to death a few weeks back, and yet they think this is a good basis <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[on which to get married?? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>And I just don’t buy the whole <i>Jesse is only like this with Ava, he isn’t at all controlling or a bastard with anyone else, just you, Ava.</i> <br><br>Lucky girl. <br><br>What a croc of shit. A person does not simply just become this controlling or downright manipulative to point of abusive with only that one person. And even if that were true, then <u>doesn’t that mean that she brings out the <i>very worst</i> in him?</u> Think on. <br><br>END OF EDIT</b><br><br>Just a note to finish on; THIS IS NOT A LOVE STORY. THESE TWO PEOPLE WILL EVENTUALLY DAMAGE EACH OTHER BEYOND REPAIR.<br><br>Will I read book Three? Yes, maybe, when I really don’t have anything better to do, just to prove to myself that this can’t get much worse, or any better.<br><br>So for now, Jesse Ward,<br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=r29mb5" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389706746ra/8049847.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>As for This Man Confessed;<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=sdfp11" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389706746ra/8049848.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/501957959" />
    <a title="Georgia ♥ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9138738-georgia"><img alt="Georgia ♥ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1377186210p2/9138738.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/501957959?book_show_action=true">Jan 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Georgia ♥ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Georgia ♥ " href="/user/show/9138738-georgia">Georgia ♥ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16156709-beneath-this-man">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=filthy-rich-hero">filthy-rich-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=in-love-with">in-love-with</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=sobbing-mess">sobbing-mess</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=lol-chuckle-worthy">lol-chuckle-worthy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=guilty-pleasures">guilty-pleasures</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=the-sound-of-my-heart-breaking">the-sound-of-my-heart-breaking</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer501957959" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16155798860507468950"><b>♥4 (no-ish) BEYOND CRAZY Stars♥</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404496ra/787146.gif' width='500' height='327' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>‘It’s pure bliss, baby. Total gratification. Absolute, complete earth shifting, universe shaking love.’</b>
</i><br/><br/>A wild ride, a rollercoaster of emotions, a train wreck and in the end catharsis... This book had it all. Also had me glued upon it, with my eyes bulging and sometimes tears running down my face or head thrown back in laughter, this book (and THIS MAN) delivered...<br/><br/>After two books I can now say for sure. There are people out there, that are broken.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404496ra/787147.gif' width='500' height='243' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Damaged, crip</span>
  <span id="freeText16155798860507468950" style="display:none"><b>♥4 (no-ish) BEYOND CRAZY Stars♥</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404496ra/787146.gif" width="500" height="327" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>‘It’s pure bliss, baby. Total gratification. Absolute, complete earth shifting, universe shaking love.’</b>
</i><br><br>A wild ride, a rollercoaster of emotions, a train wreck and in the end catharsis... This book had it all. Also had me glued upon it, with my eyes bulging and sometimes tears running down my face or head thrown back in laughter, this book (and THIS MAN) delivered...<br><br>After two books I can now say for sure. There are people out there, that are broken.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404496ra/787147.gif" width="500" height="243" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Damaged, crippled, unfunctioning. People with issues. In Jesse's case they are obvious but what took me by surprise in this book, is that apparently Ava has some too. I thought that she was just a coward running away all the time,<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401897ra/780626.gif" width="500" height="270" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>but now she is staying and she is fighting. For this relationship to work they got to find some middle group and they did. Jesse relents and Ava possesses. And they work. I'm appalled with their relationship and in love and excited. But it's them. Unique and fiercely realistic, completely crazy.<br><br><b>Ava</b><br>She left him. <br><i>
  <b> It’s been five days since I have seen Jesse Ward. Five days of agony, five days of emptiness and five days of sobbing. There is nothing left in me. No emotion, no soul and no tears – nothing.</b>
</i><br><br>But she can't stay away.... She comes back. But now she is determined. To live, to possess, to fight dirty. And she is the only one that can solve the huge enigma that is Jesse Ward.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404496ra/787148.gif" width="500" height="69" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Jesse</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404496ra/787149.gif" width="500" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>His issues, have issues. Liar and painfully truthful, dominant and submissive, insane, neurotic, crazy, possessive, vulnerable, fragile, protective, exasperating and adoring, he is one of the most complex book characters I have come across. His secrets, have secret and the only thing I'm sure, is that Ava is his salvation, his little piece of haven, his sunshine.<br><br><i>
  <b> ‘You’re mine, and mine alone, baby. Just for my eyes, just for my touch and just for my pleasure. Just mine. Do you understand me?’<br><br>‘I don’t deserve you, Ava. Not after the life I’ve lived. I’ve never had anything I’ve valued or wanted to protect. Now I have, and it’s a bizarre mixture of total happiness and complete fucking fear.’ <b></b></b>
</i><br><br>But love is actually insane and it makes sense when everything else FAILS. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404496ra/787150.gif" width="500" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>He was so unexpected, so passionate and so absolutely irresistible. And now he is wholly mine, and I am undeniably his.<br>I finally understand him.<br>I’ve finally got beneath this man.</b>
</i><br><br>No cliffhanger in this one but still many questions. Shocking and unapologetic. We got a glimpse of something terrible and there is a lot to explore. <br><br><b>Can't wait for more.... Strangely addictive and heartbreaking exciting, I've fallen for this story.</b><br><br><i>Jesse, Ava, you got it finally right, scr*w the world.... You deserve it...</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396473ra/764270.gif" width="500" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="16155798860507468950" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_471395359" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/471395359" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/471395359?book_show_action=true">Dec 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16156709-beneath-this-man">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer471395359" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13686376058578471035"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399944i/774467.jpg' width='300' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>"Your not giving me the countdown!"</i><br/><br/><b>
  <i>”Three...”</i>
</b><br/><br/><i>No Jesse I can’t stand you and Ava. Your both crazy and I’m not giving this book 4 stars!</i><br/><br/><b>
  <i>”Two...”</i>
</b><br/><br/><i>Jesse stop, where are her birth control pills?</i> <br/> <br/><b>
  <i>”One...”</i>
</b><br/><br/><i>Jesse what’s up with you and that b*tch Sara? I think you’re a hypocrite for not firing her!</i><br/><br/><b>
  <i>”Watch your mouth!”</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>”Zero...”</i>
</b><br/><br/><i>Okay, Okay Jesse you have the power and a 4 star rating. Ugh!</i><br/><br/>--------------------------------------------------------------------<br/><br/>I’ll admit it, I’m not a fan of A</span>
  <span id="freeText13686376058578471035" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399944i/774467.jpg" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>"Your not giving me the countdown!"</i><br><br><b>
  <i>”Three...”</i>
</b><br><br><i>No Jesse I can’t stand you and Ava. Your both crazy and I’m not giving this book 4 stars!</i><br><br><b>
  <i>”Two...”</i>
</b><br><br><i>Jesse stop, where are her birth control pills?</i> <br> <br><b>
  <i>”One...”</i>
</b><br><br><i>Jesse what’s up with you and that b*tch Sara? I think you’re a hypocrite for not firing her!</i><br><br><b>
  <i>”Watch your mouth!”</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>”Zero...”</i>
</b><br><br><i>Okay, Okay Jesse you have the power and a 4 star rating. Ugh!</i><br><br>--------------------------------------------------------------------<br><br>I’ll admit it, I’m not a fan of Ava O’Shea and Jesse Ward. I find them both to be absolutely crazy! I read This Man and pretty much hated their continuous loop of a craziness. He dictates power, she says no, she runs, he chases, he brings to her to submission through sex and we do it all over again. The reason why I ended up liking the first book was how it ended and the fact that I'm nosey. I’m constantly complaining about this couple. While at the same time, I’m still reading and gossiping about them. <br> <br>After the first chapter we fall right back into the loop of craziness. Jesse’s demands, Ava’s attempt at standing up for herself, and Jesse’s retribution. I’m not sure which character I despise more it maybe a tie! <br><br>Not until the last half of the book did I start to read a little quicker and get caught up in the drama. Secrets are revealed about Mr. Ward. Some are understandable and some not so understandable. The ending is not a cliffhanger, so readers can breathe easy. <br><br>Once again, the last 20 percent of the book had me hooked. I’m not on “Central Jesse Cloud Nine” but this story definitely confirms the fact that there is someone out there for everyone. I think these two deserve each other. <br><br><b>
  <i>”I love you, beyond crazy.”</i>
</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399944ra/774468.gif" width="301" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Wishing Jesse and Ava good luck in book 3. I think.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13686376058578471035" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

<span id="freeTextContainer766466442006466788">Reread on March 19th- 22nd!<br/><br/>I am so glad I have been rereading this series, I’ll have all of the details of the series for when I read Book four!<br/><br/>This is book two and I found it so much better than the first! The angst in this one made me go through so many emotions! I was so absolutely hooked on the dynamics between Eva and Jesse! I can’t wait for the newest book!! I’m onto book two now!!!</span>
