<span id="freeTextContainer2562532483567899321">I can give you four words why this book is only getting four stars.....<br/><br/><b>Watch your fucking mouth</b><br/><br/>It's <b>
  <i>that</i>
</b> much of an issue and source of contention with me. I loathe a double standard and this one really gets me all riled up. <br/><br/>The first 75% of the book is a lot of bickering back and forth and it really wore on my nerves. Just when I was getting fed up, I got totally gobsmacked. I'm talking a whole range of emotions:<br/><br/><b>I WAS SHOCKED<br/><br/><a href='http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/08f264e6cef8af850c2a51d279639cb0a829b09c_r_zps9aa88d59.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424563ra/846424.gif' alt=' photo 08f264e6cef8af850c2a51d279639cb0a829b09c_r_zps9aa88d59.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a> <br/><br/>I WAS ANGRY<br/><br/><a href='http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/Reactions/temper-tantrum-o_zpsd6b7c96b.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/529603.gif' alt=' photo temper-tantrum-o_zpsd6b7c96b.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/>I HAD TO DO A DOUBLE TAKE<br/><br/><a href='http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/Reactions/what_zps68e45592.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424563ra/846425.gif' alt=' photo what_zps68e45592.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/>I LITERALLY GOT SICK<br/><br/><a href='http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/t5gnmh_zps3129cfe3.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424563ra/846426.gif' alt=' photo t5gnmh_zps3129cfe3.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/>I WAS SPE</b></span>
  <span id="freeText2562532483567899321" style="display:none">I can give you four words why this book is only getting four stars.....<br><br><b>Watch your fucking mouth</b><br><br>It's <b>
  <i>that</i>
</b> much of an issue and source of contention with me. I loathe a double standard and this one really gets me all riled up. <br><br>The first 75% of the book is a lot of bickering back and forth and it really wore on my nerves. Just when I was getting fed up, I got totally gobsmacked. I'm talking a whole range of emotions:<br><br><b>I WAS SHOCKED<br><br><a href="http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/08f264e6cef8af850c2a51d279639cb0a829b09c_r_zps9aa88d59.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424563ra/846424.gif" alt=" photo 08f264e6cef8af850c2a51d279639cb0a829b09c_r_zps9aa88d59.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <br><br>I WAS ANGRY<br><br><a href="http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/Reactions/temper-tantrum-o_zpsd6b7c96b.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/529603.gif" alt=" photo temper-tantrum-o_zpsd6b7c96b.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>I HAD TO DO A DOUBLE TAKE<br><br><a href="http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/Reactions/what_zps68e45592.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424563ra/846425.gif" alt=" photo what_zps68e45592.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>I LITERALLY GOT SICK<br><br><a href="http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/t5gnmh_zps3129cfe3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424563ra/846426.gif" alt=" photo t5gnmh_zps3129cfe3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>I WAS SPEECHLESS<br><br><a href="http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/Favorites/shocked_WTF_zps984df4dd.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/549792.gif" alt=" photo shocked_WTF_zps984df4dd.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b><br><br>I was so emotionally and mentally stirred up I got to wondering if I was on drugs...or if I needed to be. <br><br><a href="http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/rTINQ_zps8d6e79b3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>It's clear these two are toxic to each other and they've managed to infect me with their poison.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"We make each other crazy. That's the truth of it. We're no good for each other, and he does manipulate me. The problem is, I enjoy it."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/Orgasm/tumblr_m726joF8Ie1rpfm1co1_500_zps00cf6058.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Jesse has been able to enrage me to the point of book homicide and yet he's still managed to secure a place in my heart. This man is truly something else and I'm anticipating his confession. <br></span>

<div id="review_463867989" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/463867989" />
    <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog"><img alt="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554795448p2/3870376.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/463867989?book_show_action=true">Nov 26, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog">Jenny - TotallybookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16156709-beneath-this-man">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer463867989" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1556233016494952086"><b>
  <i>CALLING ALL JESSE WARD FANS!!!! Check out all new Exclusive JESSE POV - When Jesse Turned up at Ava's - and Exclusive Giveaway you won't want to miss - check it out here at Totallybooked: </i>
</b> <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://totallybookedblog.com/2013/05/04/exclusive-jesse-ward-pov-when-jesse-turned-up-at-avas-and-giveaway/'>http://totallybookedblog.com/2013/05/...</a><br/><br/><b>J&G:</b> We suggest listening to Angel by Massive Attack while reading this review. <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=hbe3CQamF8k'>http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=hbe3CQ...</a><br/><br/><b>Gitte:</b> <b>Three…..two….One….Zero</b> …Yes Mr. Ward we are wearing Lace!!<br/><br/>I cannot even begin to say how satisfying it was to get the Lord of the Sex Manor </span>
  <span id="freeText1556233016494952086" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>CALLING ALL JESSE WARD FANS!!!! Check out all new Exclusive JESSE POV - When Jesse Turned up at Ava's - and Exclusive Giveaway you won't want to miss - check it out here at Totallybooked: </i>
</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://totallybookedblog.com/2013/05/04/exclusive-jesse-ward-pov-when-jesse-turned-up-at-avas-and-giveaway/">http://totallybookedblog.com/2013/05/...</a><br /><br /><b>J&amp;G:</b> We suggest listening to Angel by Massive Attack while reading this review. <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=hbe3CQamF8k">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=hbe3CQ...</a><br /><br /><b>Gitte:</b> <b>Three…..two….One….Zero</b> …Yes Mr. Ward we are wearing Lace!!<br /><br />I cannot even begin to say how satisfying it was to get the Lord of the Sex Manor back Jenny. I missed Mr. Jesse Ward with an aching heart. <br />He is still my number one and I will not waver on this!<br /><br />I d.e.v.o.u.r.e.d this sequel completely, I got absolutely lost in Ava and Jesse’s journey once again. It was emotional, full of suspense and angst and oh so incredibly intense and sexy! I have to say I actually enjoyed and loved Beneath This Man even more than This Man because layers were peeled and we got so much closer to these characters!!<br /><br />Some secrets come out in the open but they multiply too, so to say I am now HANGING for book #3 well that is an understatement. At least there was no cliff-hanger this time, I don’t think I could have coped with another one as I literally didn’t move for two days, I was sat on the edge of my seat lost to the world. The writing was flawless and brilliant once again and if at all possible I love both Jesse and Ava even more now!<br /><br /><b>Jenny: </b> Oh we definitely had blast off Gitte and only the best lace will do for our revisit to the one and only "how old are you?" Mr Ward! Oh and don't worry, you'll get no arguments from this end about Jesse being number one! How can you not love this intense, possessive, unreasonable, sensual, good looking, passionate and oh so very alpha, dominant man? He ticks all the fictional man boxes!<br /><br />Thankfully for me I only had to go Mr Wardless for a couple of weeks because honestly, if I'd had to wait any longer for this book after the being left with those cliff-hangers in This Man I don't think I would have been responsible for my actions! I had so many questions at the end of book one, my naturally inquisitive self was in meltdown mode. <br /><br />Luckily Gitte, we did indeed get some answers in Beneath This Man and for that I was so grateful. Then that naughty minx, Ms Malpas only goes and throws some more questions at us and here we go again, inquisitive Jenny is on the hunt! So many things I need to know, though this time, thankfully, we didn't have to contend with the "violence to the kindle" inducing cliff-hanger.<br /><br /><b>Gitte: </b> I started the continuation of Ava and Jesse’s story with tears in my eyes Jenny. The emotion of the written words leapt off the pages straight into my heart: <br /><br /><i>“I needed you and you left me”</i> – Jesse. <br /><br />Five days of “what happened?” and Ava is re-united, on dragging feet, with the shadow of the dark and broken man she cannot knowingly live or breathe without.<br /><br /><i>“My fear was completely justified; I’m lost in him again”</i> – Ava<br /><br />You know a story is going to be amazing when from page one you are hooked. The journey these two are on is so incredibly intense that the spot on sense of humour of both, the sarcasm and the situations they get into completely break it up perfectly. I have to say the scene that involves handcuffs and the elusive “How old are you” had me in absolute stitches! Oh and yeah I’ll never look at a rowing machine the same ever again!<br /><br /><b>Jenny:</b> Hmmm rowing… my new favorite hobby! Honestly Gitte, as I said to you after I finished this book, I don't think I moved…an inch….whilst reading this story! I was pulled back into the world of Jesse and Ava from the first page.<br /> <br />My heart broke from what I found five days after the turn of events at the end of This Man. They are both so broken and can't function without one another. Both in the depths of despair, suffering, in their own way, from being apart. <br /><br />In the short, yet intense relationship Ava shared with this man, he had become her reason for being, he had seared himself into her heart and then he broke it.<br /> <br />Ava tries to remain guarded and strong because she knows deep down that as soon as she sees Jesse her defenses will wither at the sight of him and knows the only chance she has to guard her heart is to keep her distance from him. Easier said than done. For reasons she can't deny, she must go to him. What she found had me feeling bereft for her. <br /><br /><b>Gitte:</b> Ava is by far one of the best if not The Best heroine out there for me. I just adore her. There’s not a single time that she has annoyed me. She is still funny, inquisitive, loves with passion and knows what’s what. She has one “weakness” and that is the enigmatic Mr. Ward…however, that is one “weakness” that is without doubt completely understandable, I think we all share that one.<br /><br /><i> “You don’t play fair Mr. Ward”</i> – Ava. <br /><br />She is fully aware that he has his very own special (and HOT) way to “manipulate” her to play along, concede and succumb; his methods totally unusual but extremely desirable and effective (umm yes please). Who’d question them? Honestly?!<br /> <br /><i>“In his words, there is not a place on my body, that hasn’t had him in it, on it or over it” </i> – Ava <br /><br />Ava has seen his dark possessive side, his vulnerable broken side and his unreasonable stubborn side but she knows this man is worth every single bit of her effort and love. He loves her fiercely, she knows this and she knows she must unravel each layer to get this man to confess it all, only then will he be wholly hers and she will understand the why’s. She knows that she cannot be without him. Her body and mind centres and moves in sync with his. Her breath and his are dependent on each other. <br /><br /><i>“Ava, you’re asking me not to touch you. That goes against all of my instincts”</i> - Jesse<br /><br /><b>Jenny:</b> I'm with you on this one too Gitte. I can't begin to tell you how I feel about Ava and how much I love her character. She has managed to bring this man to his knees.<br /><br />She has the fierce, all-consuming love of this man. Ava is a character I have become so invested in. She's human. She's not perfect, she certainly makes mistakes, she doesn't always make the right decisions and she loves Jesse so passionately, and this man is her weakness. <br /><br />She openly admits her faults and mistakes and does let Jesse push her around at times, though you can't blame her because this man is very persuasive with his sense fucks, reminder fucks and my favorite of all……the sleepy sex…oh my, even the sound of sleepy sex with Jesse gets you all fired up.<br /> <br />Ava does have a mind of her own, yet where Jesse is concerned all rational thinking flies out the window, such is the effect that man has on her, but she knows it and admits it. <br /><br />Oh but our girl doesn't let Mr Ward have his way all the time. Jesse has met his match in Ava and deep down I know he loves that about her. He challengers her and she challenges him right back and we know our Jesse loves a challenge! I love seeing these two go at it with each other. I love the times Ava stands up to Jesse, the times she gets one up on him is an absolute joy to see! <br /><br />The "age reveal" scene was brilliant! I loved it! I did wonder how that was going to come about and never in my wildest imagination would I have come up with that. That scene, for me, showed the fun and intensity of this relationship and I loved them even more because of it. I love this pair and I think I read that scene with a big stupid grin on my face!<br /><br /><b>Gitte: </b> Now Jesse, seriously where do I even begin? This man is just imperfectly perfect. A true lovable rogue!<br /><br /><i>“You’re mine, and mine alone, baby. Just for my eyes, just for my touch and just for my pleasure. Just Mine. Do you understand me?”</i> – Jesse<br /><br />We learn more about this gorgeous, cocky domineering man in this sequel. We learn of his vulnerability, his power, his drive and snippets from his past.<br /><br />And yeah even the elusive age! He is just as frustrating and demanding as in This Man, perhaps even more so, because he nearly lost Ava and he refuses to ever be in that situation again. He loves her so fiercely and passionately that he is afraid to lose control…indeed to lose her; so he does whatever he can to ensure she understands that she is his and he is hers. <br /> <br /><i>“I knew you were the one the second I laid eyes on you” </i>– Jesse<br /><br /><i>“How did you know?”</i> – Ava<br /><br /><i>“Because my heart started beating again.”</i> – Jesse<br /><br /><b>Jenny:</b> Ah Mr Ward, he's still a mystery but little by little we're stripping away the layers and learning more and more about this rather complicated man, and I am loving every minute of it! Oh there were times he frustrated me! Nearly losing this woman has driven him to the point of distraction and for a man who is used to being in total control of everything in his life, Ava has turned his world upside down. <br /><br />Now, as much as Ava loses all rationality where Jesse is concerned, it's definitely not a one way street. This man can hardly think straight as far as Ava is concerned, the fear of losing her consumes him, which makes for very interesting times on both sides. <br /> <br /><b>Gitte:</b> So we still have so many mysterious threads still unsolved Jenny…we have mysterious women, hidden drama waiting in the wings, un-confessed confessions and pasts waiting to be explored and I cannot for the life of me wait to find out exactly what is going on. <br /><br />And yeah…I didn’t just love’ish Beneath This Man…I LOVED IT and cannot wait for the last installment in Jesse and Ava’s journey! Oh and the ending….SIGH….The ending!!!<br /><br /><b>Jenny:</b> I know I've driven you crazy with my theories Gitte, but I'm giving you advance warning that I am not giving up until book three, This Man Confessed, is in my hot little hands. What about…..hmmm we can't discuss that 'cause it's a spoiler….and then…..nope, another spoiler!<br /><br />So, what did I think of Beneath This Man? I bloody LOVED it. I loved every twist and turn. I loved the "off the charts" steam factor in this book. I love the chemistry and passion between Jesse and Ava and I loved the mystery that still surrounds their lives. <br /><br />Yes, I loved every frustrating second, I loved Jesse and Ava even more and yes, the end of this book completely satisfied me. <br /><br />What a great follow up to This Man. I really do hope Jodi Ellen Malpas is madly typing away at that third book as we speak because I need it NOW! <br /><br /><i>ARC given by the author for an honest review</i></span>

  <span id="freeText10414897276453238688" style="display:none">The Lord of the Sex Manor Mr Jesse Ward is the sex god that Ava must have and run away from in the same manner. Now everyone sees Jesse's achilles they all now want a piece of Ava to make Jesse pay for all his past sin that he never cared for or who he mowed over to get there. <div id="review_776525605" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/776525605" />
    <a title="Catarina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina"><img alt="Catarina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514808293p2/11538033.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/776525605?book_show_action=true">Nov 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catarina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catarina" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina">Catarina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=is-getting-hot-in-here">is-getting-hot-in-here</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer776525605" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6053802697491430561"> <b>4 Crazy-ish Stars</b>	<br/><br/>This second installment starts five days after Ava found out about Jesse's lifestyle and job. She was obviously not happy about it. <br/>But Jesse has an even worse reaction to her exit and drowns himself in sorrow and alcohol. He just wants her back. <br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385949673i/7264112.jpg' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>But after that happens (No. This isn’t a spoiler. It’s pretty obvious, otherwise wouldn’t be THREE books.), things aren’t automatically easy and perfect. Jesse's past keeps coming in their way and Ava is starting to get a little (lit</span>
  <span id="freeText6053802697491430561" style="display:none"> <b>4 Crazy-ish Stars</b>	<br><br>This second installment starts five days after Ava found out about Jesse's lifestyle and job. She was obviously not happy about it. <br>But Jesse has an even worse reaction to her exit and drowns himself in sorrow and alcohol. He just wants her back. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385949673i/7264112.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But after that happens (No. This isn’t a spoiler. It’s pretty obvious, otherwise wouldn’t be THREE books.), things aren’t automatically easy and perfect. Jesse's past keeps coming in their way and Ava is starting to get a little (little being an understatement) neurotic about it. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385949673ra/7264113.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In this second book we have them trying to figure out each other and living with their differences, hoping for a future when their past keeps haunting them, and a lot of people try to separate them. <br>They’re the ones controlling their lives and their love… but what can happen when they lose all of it? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385949673i/7264114.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If I thought the previous book was crazy… then this definitely takes the prize. This couple is completely bat-sh*t crazy. <br>They are fighting and screaming at each other in a second and in the next one they are doing it like bunnies. <br>I love how Ava doesn’t take anything from him. She fights back and likes to play dirty. Although she is easily coerced. (Who wouldn’t be?).<br>And with Jesse's past, his craziness and possessiveness, I still love him. He’s sexy and a completely passionate man. Even being his first time feeling that way. But I get the feeling that there’s much more to his past than we are getting from him. <br>So, I can’t wait for the final book and finally see how this crazy love story will end. ;) </span>
  <a data-text-id="6053802697491430561" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1412978267" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3286968978660251110"><b>☆☆4 Jesse Ward is the MAN Stars☆☆</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445312748i/16629970._SY540_.jpg' width='380' height='360' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445313123i/16630087._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Coming straight off of book one (with my low rating), I'm surprised that I even started book 2. My friends told me not to give up on Jesse and I'm so glad I didn't! So many secrets were uncovered and I felt like so many layers of Jesse was revealed. <i>He's truly unlike any hero I've ever read</i>. When I thought I knew him, I'm hit with another surprise. I'm glad to say he's definitely grown on me. <br/><br/>I loved the back and forth bantering between Jesse and Ava. Their dynam</span>
  <span id="freeText3286968978660251110" style="display:none"><b>☆☆4 Jesse Ward is the MAN Stars☆☆</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445312748i/16629970._SY540_.jpg" width="380" height="360" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445313123i/16630087._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Coming straight off of book one (with my low rating), I'm surprised that I even started book 2. My friends told me not to give up on Jesse and I'm so glad I didn't! So many secrets were uncovered and I felt like so many layers of Jesse was revealed. <i>He's truly unlike any hero I've ever read</i>. When I thought I knew him, I'm hit with another surprise. I'm glad to say he's definitely grown on me. <br><br>I loved the back and forth bantering between Jesse and Ava. Their dynamic is funny, intense, combustible, heated and sensual. Jesse is being changed, but so is Ava in her own little way. Yes this book was a bit wordy at times, but I enjoyed every minute of it. <br><br></span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Vb8KRqXjGdl4W7pqQCrKzQcDBDidmBcxKlxMxEiehdZvmWOUHr3Qsd9wDgu338AS0Vzj8FMVmVZxIgp1hd13TA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('H7vFCWmliSzA1vWqSwX6joMCgVsZjLrnOnAiUBd07/Ulnazb0vtARGf9Qcu88PBRVV1mk9cBNIBhDmTh2jcdbw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer4425337136330000631">‘A lingering idea that I just couldn’t ignore.’ – Jodi Ellen Malpas<br/><br/>Jodi Ellen Malpas wrote her debut series, The This Man Trilogy, in secret, worried about what people might think if they knew what her imagination was capable of. She was shocked herself. But she finally found the courage to unleash her creative streak and self-published THIS MAN - the first book of the This Man Trilogy - in Octobe</span>
  <span id="freeText4425337136330000631" style="display:none">‘A lingering idea that I just couldn’t ignore.’ – Jodi Ellen Malpas<br /><br />Jodi Ellen Malpas wrote her debut series, The This Man Trilogy, in secret, worried about what people might think if they knew what her imagination was capable of. She was shocked herself. But she finally found the courage to unleash her creative streak and self-published THIS MAN - the first book of the This Man Trilogy - in October 2012. She took a chance on a story with a hero who soon became one of modern day fictions most prolific alpha male characters. <br /><br />Jesse Ward – also affectionately known as The Lord of The Manor, sparked incredible reactions from women across the globe and catapulted Jodi into the world of women’s fiction. With so much love and enthusiasm from her readers, and a thirst for more of her words, Jodi suddenly wasn't afraid of her imagination anymore. She went on to write The One Night Trilogy with the delectable and mysterious Miller Hart, and stole the hearts of her readers once again. She’s now a proud #1 New York Times bestselling author – all six of her published novels having hit the New York Times best sellers list – as well as a Sunday Times bestseller and international best seller. Her work is published in over 20 languages across the world. <br /><br />Jodi was born and raised in the Midlands town of Northampton, England, where she lives with her two boys and a beagle. She is a self-professed daydreamer, a Converse &amp; mojito addict, and has a terrible weak spot for Alpha Males.<br /><br />Writing powerful love stories and creating addictive characters has become her passion – a passion she now shares with her devoted readers<br /></span>
